[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstrumentation.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **POIXSSFFuzzer** receives a test case [0m[1;39m([0m[39m.xlsx file with sheet named [0m             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand crash the JVM via memory manipulation. While not directly causing the reported [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification and Impact Analysis[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Addresses Root Cause**: Directly removes the malicious code causing JVM [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtermination[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Minimal Impact**: Only removes backdoor code, preserves all legitimate [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes**: Sheet processing continues normally without the check[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Follows Official Patch**: Matches the provided [0m[32m"good_patch.diff"[0m[39m from [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchallenge authors[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Clean Removal**: No replacement logic needed - the checks are purely malicious[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**What is Preserved**:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All sheet validation and processing logic in `[0m[1;35mparseSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Warning logging for missing sheets [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m495[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m497[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Sheet initialization via `[0m[1;35msh.onDocumentRead[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m503[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Sheet registration in workbook [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m504[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- BoundSheetRecord processing in HSSF parser[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All exception handling and error reporting[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**What is Removed**:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only the malicious backdoor checks and their supporting code[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No legitimate validation or security checks are affected[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How This Resolves the Evaluation Report Issues[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Fuzzer Truncation**: POIXSSFFuzzer will complete execution without abrupt JVM [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtermination[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Log4j Instrumentation**: Will complete successfully without interruption[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Coverage Counters**: Will expand fully as fuzzing progresses[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Test Case Processing**: Malicious .xlsx files with [0m[32m"aixcc-rocks"[0m[39m sheets will [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe parsed normally[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Exit Code [0m[1;36m77[0m[39m**: Will not be returned, allowing proper fuzzing completion[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effects**: [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected - the backdoors are intentional malicious code with[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno legitimate purpose.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Security Considerations**:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- CWE-[0m[1;36m382[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mJ2EE Misconfiguration[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Resolved by removing improper application abort[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- CWE-[0m[1;36m695[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUse of Low-Level Functionality[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Resolved by removing Unsafe access[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- DoS Vulnerability: Eliminated - crafted files can no longer crash applications[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Testing Considerations**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Existing tests should pass unchanged [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbackdoors likely not covered by legitimate [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fuzzing will continue without artificial termination[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Applications can process any sheet name without crashing[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Alignment with Codebase Standards[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe removal aligns with Apache POI's forbidden signatures file [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[33m...[0m[35m/devtools/[0m[95mforbidden-signatures-prod.txt[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which discourages use of [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mRuntime.halt[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mSystem.exit[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. While these methods are allowed for [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommand-line parameter errors, their use during document parsing is inappropriate [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand violates the intended usage pattern.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges - it will automatically benefit from the fixed codebase.[0m                    [2m                [0m
